It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_CHANNEL = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per token. It's computed on-the-fly.\n    PER_TOKEN = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per group. It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_GROUP = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in INT8.\n    INT8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in FP8.\n    FP8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # FP8 QDQ\n    FP8_QDQ = auto()\n    # FP8 rowwise\n    FP8_ROWWISE = auto()\n    # FP8 block scales for Deepseek\n    FP8_1x128_128x128 = auto()\n    # W4A8 qserve\n    W4A8_QSERVE = auto()\n    # FP4\n    NVFP4 = auto()\n    NVFP4_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # W4A8 NVFP4\n    W4A8_NVFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    # W4A8 MXFP4\n    W4A8_MXFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8 = auto()\n    W4A16_MXFP4 = auto()\n\n    # The smallest power-of-two that is not used by a flag. You can restrict the test to the bits indicated by \"mask\".\n    def _all(self, bits, mask=VALID_FLAGS):\n        return (self & mask) == bits\n\n    # Is one of the bits of the mask set?\n    def _any(self, bits):\n        return (self & bits) != 0\n\n    def is_int8_weight_only(self):\n        return self._all(self.INT8_WEIGHTS, self.WEIGHTS_AND_ACTIVATIONS)\n\n    def is_int4_weight_only(self):\n        return self._all(self.INT4_WEIGHTS, self.WEIGHTS_AND_ACTIVATIONS)\n\n    def is_weight_only(self):\n        return self.is_int4_weight_only() or | self.NVFP4_KV_CACHE)\n\n    def set_int8_kv_cache(self):\n        return self | self.INT8_KV_CACHE\n\n    def set_fp8_kv_cache(self):\n        return self | self.FP8_KV_CACHE\n\n    def ValueError(f\"Unsupported combination of QuantMode args: \"\n                             f\"{quantize_weights=}, \"\n                             f\"{quantize_activations=}, \"\n                f\"{use_int8_kv_cache=}, \"\n                             f\"{use_fp8_kv_cache=}, \"\n                             f\"{use_fp8_qdq=}, \"\n                       f\"{use_w4a8_mxfp4_fp8=}, \"\n                             f\"{use_w4a8_mxfp4_mxfp8=}, \"\n                             f\"{use_w4a16_mxfp4=}\")\n\n        # We must quantize weights when we quantize activations.\n        if quantize_activations and not quantize_weights:\n            raise_error()\n\n        # If we set per_token or per_channel, we must quantize both weights and activations.\n        if (per_token or per_channel) and not (quantize_weights\n                                               and quantize_activations):\n            raise_error()\n\n        mode = QuantMode(0)\n\n        # Do we quantize the weights - if so, do we use INT4 or INT8?\n        if quantize_weights and use_int4_weights:\n            mode = mode | QuantMode.INT4_WEIGHTS\n        elif quantize_weights:\n            mode = mode | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n\n        # Do we quantize the activations?\n        if quantize_activations:\n            mode = mode | QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS\n\n        # Per-channel/per-token/per-group additional flags.\n        if per_channel:\n            mode = mode | QuantMode.PER_CHANNEL\n        if per_token:\n            mode = mode | QuantMode.PER_TOKEN\n        if per_group:\n            mode = mode | QuantMode.PER_GROUP\n\n        # Int8 KV cache\n        if use_int8_kv_cache:\n            mode = mode | It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_CHANNEL = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per token. It's computed on-the-fly.\n    PER_TOKEN = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per group. It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_GROUP = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in INT8.\n    INT8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in FP8.\n    FP8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # FP8 QDQ\n    FP8_QDQ = auto()\n    # FP8 rowwise\n    FP8_ROWWISE = auto()\n    # FP8 block scales for Deepseek\n    FP8_1x128_128x128 = auto()\n    # W4A8 qserve\n    W4A8_QSERVE = auto()\n    # FP4\n    NVFP4 = auto()\n    NVFP4_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # W4A8 NVFP4\n    W4A8_NVFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    # W4A8 MXFP4\n    W4A8_MXFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    W4A8_MXFP4_INT8 = auto()\n    W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8 = auto()\n    W4A16_MXFP4 = auto()\n\n    # The smallest power-of-two that is not used by a flag. Fallback to tempdir\n    53→        tmp_dir = Path(tempfile.gettempdir())\n    54→        tmp_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n    55→        tmp_lock_path = tmp_dir / \"_remote_code.lock\"\n    56→        tmp_lock = filelock.FileLock(str(tmp_lock_path), timeout=timeout)\n    57→        try:\n    58→            with tmp_lock:\n    59→                yield\n    60→        except filelock.Timeout:\n    61→            logger.warning(\n    62→                f\"failed to acquire tempdir config lock within {timeout} seconds, proceeding without lock\"\n    63→            )\n    64→            # proceed without lock\n    65→            yield\n    66→        except (PermissionError) as e:\n    67→            logger.warning(\n    68→                f\"tempdir config lock unavailable due to OS/permission issue: {e}, proceeding without lock\"\n    69→            )\n    70→            # proceed without lock\n    71→            yield\n    72→\n    73→\n    74→@dataclass(kw_only=True)\n    75→class ModelConfig(Generic[TConfig]):\n    76→    pretrained_config: Optional[TConfig] = None\n    77→    mapping: Mapping = field(default_factory=Mapping)\n    78→\n    79→    # Quantization configs\n    80→    quant_config: QuantConfig = field(default_factory=QuantConfig)\n    81→    # Per linear layer quantization in quant_cfg.json or hf_quant_config.json\n    82→    quant_config_dict: Optional[Dict[str, QuantConfig]] = None\n    83→    # All rights reserved.\n# SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\n#\n# Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the \"License\");\n# you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.\n# You may obtain a copy of the License at\n#\n# http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n#\n# Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n# distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n# WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n# See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n# limitations under the License.\nimport unittest\n\nfrom tensorrt_llm.quantization import QuantMode\n\n\nclass TestQuantMode(unittest.TestCase):\n\n    def test_all(self):\n        # Set activations and weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n\n        # Make sure _all returns True when asked for both ACTIVATIONS and INT8_WEIGHTS.\n        self.assertTrue(qm._all(QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS))\n        # Make sure _all returns False when asked only for ACTIVATIONS.\n        self.assertFalse(qm._all(QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS))\n        # Make sure _all returns True when asked only for ACTIVATIONS if limited to ACTIVATIONS flag.\n        self.assertTrue(\n            qm._all(QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS, mask=QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS))\n\n    def test_any(self):\n        # Set activations and weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n\n        # Make sure _any returns True when asked for both ACTIVATIONS and INT8_WEIGHTS.\n        self.assertTrue(qm._any(QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS))\n        # Make sure _any returns True when asked only for ACTIVATIONS.\n        self.assertTrue(qm._any(QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS))\n        # Make sure _any returns False when asked for PER_TOKEN.\n        self.assertFalse(qm._any(QuantMode.PER_TOKEN))\n\n    def test_count(self):\n        # Make sure the COUNT value is as expected - change that test if you add a new flag.\n        self.assertEqual(QuantMode.COUNT.value, 1 << 18)\n\n    def test_from_description(self):\n        # Test weight only.\n        qm = QuantMode.from_description(True, False, False, False)\n        # Make sure only the INT8_WEIGHTS flag is set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS)\n\n        # Test weight only.\n        qm = QuantMode.use_weight_only()\n        # Make sure only the INT8_WEIGHTS flag is set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS)\n\n        # Test weight only (int4).\n        qm = QuantMode.from_description(True, False, False, False, False, True)\n        # Make sure only the INT4_WEIGHTS flag is set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, QuantMode.INT4_WEIGHTS)\n\n        # Test weight only.\n        qm = QuantMode.use_weight_only(use_int4_weights=True)\n        # Make sure only the INT4_WEIGHTS flag is set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, QuantMode.INT4_WEIGHTS)\n\n        # Test activation/weight per-tensor.\n        qm = QuantMode.from_description(True, True, False, False)\n        # The reference.\n        expected_qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure ACTIVATIONS and INT8_WEIGHTS flags are set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, expected_qm)\n\n        # Test activation/weight per-tensor.\n        qm = QuantMode.use_smooth_quant()\n        # Make sure ACTIVATIONS and INT8_WEIGHTS flags are set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, expected_qm)\n\n        # Test activation/weight per-tensor & per-channel.\n        qm = QuantMode.from_description(True, True, False, True)\n        # The reference.\n        expected_qm = expected_qm | QuantMode.PER_CHANNEL\n        # Make sure ACTIVATIONS, INT8_WEIGHTS and PER_CHANNEL flags are set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, expected_qm)\n\n        # Test activation/weight per-tensor & per-channel.\n        qm = QuantMode.use_smooth_quant(per_channel=True)\n        # Make sure ACTIVATIONS, INT8_WEIGHTS and PER_CHANNEL flags are set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, expected_qm)\n\n        # Test activation/weight per-token & per-channel.\n        qm = QuantMode.from_description(True, True, True, True)\n        # The expected result.\n        expected_qm = expected_qm | QuantMode.PER_TOKEN\n        # Make sure all flags are set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, expected_qm)\n\n        # Test activation/weight per-token & per-channel.\n        qm = QuantMode.use_smooth_quant(True, True)\n        # Make sure all flags are set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, expected_qm)\n\n    def test_per_channel(self):\n        # Set per-channel flag.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS | QuantMode.PER_CHANNEL\n        # Make sure it returns True for per-channel.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_per_channel_scaling())\n        # Do not set per-channel flag.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns False for per-channel.\n        self.assertFalse(qm.has_per_channel_scaling())\n\n    def test_per_token(self):\n        # Set per-token flag.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS | QuantMode.PER_TOKEN\n        # Make sure it returns True for per-token.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_per_token_dynamic_scaling())\n        # Make sure it returns False for per-tensor.\n        self.assertFalse(qm.has_act_static_scaling())\n\n        # Do not set per-token flag.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns False for per-token.\n        self.assertFalse(qm.has_per_token_dynamic_scaling())\n        # Make sure it returns True for per-tensor.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_act_static_scaling())\n\n    def test_weights_only(self):\n        # Set weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_weight_only())\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_int8_weight_only())\n\n        # Set weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.INT4_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_weight_only())\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_int4_weight_only())\n\n        # Set activations and weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns False for weight-only.\n        self.assertFalse(qm.is_weight_only())\n\n    def test_int8_kv_cache(self):\n        # Set int8 kv cache flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.INT8_KV_CACHE\n        # Make sure it returns True for kv_cache.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_int8_kv_cache())\n        # Make sure it returns True for any quantization.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_any_quant())\n\n        # Set weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns True for any quantization.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_any_quant())\n        # Set int8 KV cache flag.\n        qm = qm.set_int8_kv_cache()\n        # Make sure it returns True for kv_cache.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_int8_kv_cache())\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_weight_only())\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_int8_weight_only())\n\n    def test_failure_quant(self):\n        # Expect failure if weights are not quantized, but activations are.\n        self.assertRaises(\n            ValueError,\n            lambda: QuantMode.from_description(False, True, False, False))\n\n        # Expect failure if per token and per channel quantization, but weights and activations are not quantized.\n        self.assertRaises(\n            ValueError,\n            lambda: QuantMode.from_description(False, False, True, True))\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    unittest.main()\n","numLines":186,"startLine":1,"totalLines":186}}}
